Created attachment 645831
patch v1

To prepare for the sub-test that covers userTypedValue, we call setBrowserState() and pass an empty session to it. That means we're actually restoring a session.

While the single blank tab is still loading, _collectTabData() still returns the tab's restore data because it's not fully restored, yet. Thus we need to wait for it to load until we can compare the value returned by getBrowserState() to the expected values.

We need to keep the executeSoon() here so that the test doesn't fail because we rely on a specific order of registered event handlers.
